<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">List of Wikipedias</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
<div id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
<div id="contentSub"><span class="mw-redirectedfrom">  (Redirected from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/index.php?title=Gothic_Wikipedia&amp;redirect=no" title="Gothic Wikipedia">Gothic Wikipedia</a>)</span></div>
<div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
					Jump to:					<a href="#mw-head">navigation</a>, 					<a href="#p-search">search</a>
</div>
<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><script>function mfTempOpenSection(id){var block=document.getElementById("mf-section-"+id);block.className+=" open-block";block.previousSibling.className+=" open-block";}</script><div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Www.wikipedia.org_screenshot_2013.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1710" data-file-width="1779" height="211" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Www.wikipedia.org_screenshot_2013.png/220px-Www.wikipedia.org_screenshot_2013.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Www.wikipedia.org_screenshot_2013.png/330px-Www.wikipedia.org_screenshot_2013.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e9/Www.wikipedia.org_screenshot_2013.png/440px-Www.wikipedia.org_screenshot_2013.png 2x" width="220"/></a>

<p>This is a list of the different language editions of <b><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a></b>; as of 25 January 2017 there are 295 Wikipedias of which 284 are active.</p>
<p></p>

</div>
</div>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">See also: <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wikimedia_projects#Language_codes" title="Wikimedia projects">Wikimedia projects § Language codes</a></div>
<p>Each Wikipedia has a code, which is used as a subdomain below wikipedia.org. Interlanguage links are sorted by that code. The codes represent the language codes defined by <a href="/wiki/ISO_639-1" title="ISO 639-1">ISO 639-1</a> and <a href="/wiki/ISO_639-3" title="ISO 639-3">ISO 639-3</a>, and the decision of which language code to use is usually determined by the <a href="/wiki/IETF_language_tag" title="IETF language tag">IETF language tag</a> policy. Wikipedias also vary by how thinly they slice dialects and variants; for example, the English Wikipedia includes most modern varieties of English (American English, Indian English, South African English, etc.), but does not include other related languages such as <a href="/wiki/Scots_language" title="Scots language">Scots</a>, or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anglo-Saxon_language" title="Anglo-Saxon language">Anglo-Saxon</a>, all of which have separate Wikipedias. The Spanish Wikipedia includes both <a href="/wiki/Castilian_Spanish" title="Castilian Spanish">Peninsular Castilian</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Latin_American_Spanish" title="Latin American Spanish">Latin American Spanish</a>; Malay Wikipedia includes a large number of Malay languages; and so on.</p>
<p>Differences between the ISO mappings and Wikipedia codes include:</p>
<table class="wikitable sortable">
<tr>
<th>WP edition name</th>
<th>WP code</th>
<th>Code meaning in ISO 639</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Albanian_language" title="Albanian language">Albanian</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://sq.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="sq:">sq</a></td>
<td>'sq' is the ISO code for the Albanian macrolanguage that includes four individual languages, although <a href="/wiki/Tosk_Albanian" title="Tosk Albanian">Tosk Albanian</a> is mainly used. 'Als' is the individual code for Tosk Albanian, but this code is used for <a href="/wiki/Alemannic_Wikipedia" title="Alemannic Wikipedia">Alemannic Wikipedia</a>.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Alemannic_German" title="Alemannic German">Alemannic</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://als.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="als:">als</a></td>
<td>'als' is the ISO code for <a href="/wiki/Tosk_Albanian" title="Tosk Albanian">Tosk Albanian</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> ISO doesn't map exactly here; 'gsw' is the ISO 639-2 and -3 code for <a href="/wiki/Swiss_German" title="Swiss German">Swiss German</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alemannic_German" title="Alemannic German">Alemannic German</a>, and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Alsatian_language" title="Alsatian language">Alsatian</a>. 'gct' is the ISO 639-3 code for <a href="/wiki/Colonia_Tovar_dialect" title="Colonia Tovar dialect">Colonia Tovar dialect</a>, 'swg' is for <a href="/wiki/Swabian_German" title="Swabian German">Swabian German</a>, and 'wae' is for <a href="/wiki/Walser_German" title="Walser German">Walser German</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Aromanian_language" title="Aromanian language">Aromanian</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://roa-rup.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="roa-rup:">roa-rup</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code. 'roa' is Romance (Other); ISO uses 'rup'.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Banyumasan_language" title="Banyumasan language">Banyumasan</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://map-bms.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="map-bms:">map-bms</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code. 'map' is Austronesian (Other).</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Dutch_Low_Saxon" title="Dutch Low Saxon">Dutch Low Saxon</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://nds-nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="nds-nl:">nds-nl</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code. nds is 'Low Saxon', restricted to Germany in Ethnologue. The Low Saxon dialects in the Netherlands have their own ISO codes.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Bihari_languages" title="Bihari languages">Bihari</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://bh.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="bh:">bh</a></td>
<td>ISO collective code 'bih' is a macrolanguage which includes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bhojpuri" title="Bhojpuri">Bhojpuri</a> (bho), <a href="/wiki/Maithili_language" title="Maithili language">Maithili</a> (mai), <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Magahi" title="Magahi">Magahi</a> (mag) and nine others<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> Bihari Wikipedia excludes <a href="/wiki/Maithili_language" title="Maithili language">Maithili</a> (<a class="extiw" href="https://mai.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="mai:">mai</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Fiji_Hindi" title="Fiji Hindi">Fiji Hindi</a> (<a class="extiw" href="https://hif.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="hif:">hif</a>) which exist as independent Wikipedias.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cantonese_language" title="Cantonese language">Cantonese</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://zh-yue.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="zh-yue:">zh-yue</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code; ISO uses 'yue'.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Classical_Chinese" title="Classical Chinese">Classical Chinese</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://zh-classical.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="zh-classical:">zh-classical</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code; ISO uses 'lzh'.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Malay_language" title="Malay language">Malay</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://ms.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="ms:">ms</a></td>
<td>Macro language that includes more than <a href="/wiki/Malayan_languages" title="Malayan languages">30 individual languages and dialects</a>. However, the wiki excludes <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_language" title="Indonesian language">Indonesian</a> because <a href="/wiki/Indonesian_Wikipedia" title="Indonesian Wikipedia">Indonesian Wikipedia</a> (<a class="extiw" href="https://id.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="id:">id</a>) exists independently.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Min_Nan" title="Min Nan">Min Nan</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://zh-min-nan.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="zh-min-nan:">zh-min-nan</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code; ISO uses 'nan'.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Bokm%C3%A5l" title="Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://no.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="no:">no</a></td>
<td>ISO uses <i>no</i> for Norwegian in general. Bokmal specifically is 'nb' or 'nob'. (Norwegian Nynorsk is at 'nn' in both ISO and Wikipedia.)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Ripuarian_language" title="Ripuarian language">Ripuarian</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://ksh.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="ksh:">ksh</a></td>
<td>ISO ksh is for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/K%C3%B6lsch_language" title="Kölsch language">Kölsch language</a>, the most prominent dialect of the Ripuarian language group. The other variants (e.g. the <a href="/wiki/Aachen_dialect" title="Aachen dialect">Aachen dialect</a>) do not have ISO codes.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Samogitian_dialect" title="Samogitian dialect">Samogitian</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://bat-smg.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="bat-smg:">bat-smg</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code; ISO uses 'sgs'. 'bat' is Baltic (Other).</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Basic_English" title="Basic English">Simple English</a></td>
<td>simple</td>
<td>Not an ISO code.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tarantino_language" title="Tarantino language">Tarantino</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://roa-tara.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="roa-tara:">roa-tara</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code. 'roa' is Romance (Other).</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/V%C3%B5ro_language" title="Võro language">Võro</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://fiu-vro.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="fiu-vro:">fiu-vro</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code; ISO uses 'vro'.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td><a href="/wiki/Chavacano" title="Chavacano">Zamboanga Chavacano</a></td>
<td><a class="extiw" href="https://cbk-zam.wikipedia.org/wiki/" title="cbk-zam:">cbk-zam</a></td>
<td>Not an ISO code; ISO uses 'cbk' as Chavacano.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p>Additionally, Wikipedias vary in <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/orthography" title="wikt:orthography">wikt:orthography</a> at times. <a href="/wiki/Chinese_Wikipedia" title="Chinese Wikipedia">Chinese Wikipedia</a> automatically translates from modern <a href="/wiki/Mandarin_Chinese" title="Mandarin Chinese">Mandarin Chinese</a> into four standard forms: Mainland China and Singapore in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Simplified_Chinese" title="Simplified Chinese">simplified Chinese</a> characters, and Taiwan and Hong Kong / Macau in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Traditional_Chinese" title="Traditional Chinese">traditional Chinese</a> characters. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Belarussian_language" title="Belarussian language">Belarussian</a>, however, has a separate Wikipedia for the 'normative' orthography (be) and <a href="/wiki/Tara%C5%A1kievica" title="Taraškievica">Taraškievica</a> (be-tarask).</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="List">List</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Wikipedias&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: List">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>An approximation to the number of active users is given in powers of ten (see <a href="/wiki/Common_logarithm" title="Common logarithm">common logarithm</a>): so "5" means at least 10,000, "4" means at least 1000, "3" means at least 100, and so on.</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Detailed_list">Detailed list</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Wikipedias&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Detailed list">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Wikipedias&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>The "<b>Total</b>" column refers to the number of pages in <i>all</i> namespaces, including both <b>articles</b> (the <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:What_is_an_article%3F" title="Wikipedia:What is an article?">official article count</a> of each wiki) and <b>non-articles</b> (user pages, images, talk pages, "project" pages, categories, and templates).</li>
<li>"<b>Active Users</b>" are registered users who have made at least one edit in the last thirty days.</li>
<li>"<b>Images</b>" is the number of locally uploaded files. Note that some large Wikipedias don't use local images and rely on <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_Commons" title="Wikimedia Commons">Commons</a> completely, so the value 0 is not a glitch.</li>
<li>The "<b><a class="extiw" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia_article_depth" title="m:Wikipedia article depth">Depth</a></b>" column (<b>Edits/Articles × Non-Articles/Articles × [1−Stub-ratio]</b>) is a rough indicator of a Wikipedia’s quality, showing how frequently its articles are updated. It does not refer to <i>academic</i> quality.</li>
</ul>

<th scope="col">Admins</th>

<th scope="col">Active Users</th>
<th scope="col">Images</th>
<th scope="col">Depth</th>
</tr>
